# Welcome! | Cyberdrop-DL

Cyberdrop-DL is an open source asynchronous downloader maintained by [jbsparrowarrow-up-right](https://github.com/jbsparrow)
. It's goal is to act as a bulk downloader for various sites you will find around the web.

[globe-pointerSupported Websiteschevron-right](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/reference/supported-websites)

[hashtag](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl#want-to-jump-right-in)

Want to jump right in?


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Explore the Getting Started guide to quickly familiarize yourself with the setup process and get started with the software.

[bullseye-arrowGetting Startedchevron-right](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/getting-started)

[hashtag](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl#want-to-customize-your-experience)

Want to customize your experience?


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Take a closer look and begin exploring the available configuration options and CLI arguments:

[slidersConfiguration Optionschevron-right](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/reference/configuration-options)
[rectangle-terminalCLI Argumentschevron-right](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/reference/cli-arguments)
[envelope-open-textNotificationschevron-right](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/reference/notifications)

[NextGetting Startedchevron-right](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/getting-started)

# Getting Started | Cyberdrop-DL

[hashtag](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/getting-started#installing-cyberdrop-dl)

Installing Cyberdrop-DL


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

There are two ways to install Cyberdrop-DL. The first is the easy method, where you simply download the start scripts. The start scripts will automatically install a compatible python version and then install Cyberdrop-DL.

The second method is installing cyberdrop-dl directly from pypi using `uv`, `pipx` or `pip`

For instructions, see:

[downloadCyberdrop-DL Installchevron-right](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/getting-started/cyberdrop-dl-install)
[androidRunning CDL on Androidchevron-right](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/getting-started/cyberdrop-dl-on-android)

[hashtag](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/getting-started#what-now)

What now?


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

If you downloaded the start scripts, just open the start script with the name of the OS you are using. For a manual install, execute the program with this command:

Copy

    cyberdrop-dl-patched

On the main screen, you can use the 'Edit URLs' option to add the URLs for the files you wish to download, them select the `download` option. That's it!

However, Cyberdrop-DL has a ton of configuration options if you want more control over the downloads. You may want to review the following:

[slidersConfiguration Optionschevron-right](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/reference/configuration-options)
[rectangle-terminalCLI Argumentschevron-right](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/reference/cli-arguments)
[envelope-open-textNotificationschevron-right](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/reference/notifications)

By default, all config files are under the `AppData` folder, which is created on the same directory that CDL it run from.

You may also want to peek at what websites the program actually supports:

[globe-pointerSupported Websiteschevron-right](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/reference/supported-websites)

If you have any issues, perhaps the [FAQ](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/frequently-asked-questions)
 might help you!

[PreviousWelcome!chevron-left](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl)
[NextCyberdrop-DL Installchevron-right](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/getting-started/cyberdrop-dl-install)

Last updated 5 months ago

# Cyberdrop-DL Install | Cyberdrop-DL

[hashtag](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/getting-started/cyberdrop-dl-install#using-start-scripts-from-release-page)

Using Start Scripts (From Release Page)


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

This is the simplest method to get the program up and running. Pre-configured start files are provided that will automatically install python, install cyberdrop-dl, update, and launch the program for you.

circle-info

The start scripts only work on 64bits operating systems. If you are running a 32bit OS, you need to install directly from pypi and may need to compile some dependencies

You can download them here: [https://github.com/jbsparrow/CyberDropDownloader/releases/latestarrow-up-right](https://github.com/jbsparrow/CyberDropDownloader/releases/latest)

You only need to download the `Cyberdrop-DL_<version>.zip` file, you don't need to worry about the other files.

Extract the contents of the zip file to any location where you'd like the program to run and store downloaded files. The extracted files will include a start file for Windows, macOS, and Linux

If you're using Windows or Linux, simply open the start file, and it will handle the rest for you

circle-info

If you are using Windows, **DO NOT** run the script as admin

On macOS, you should be able to open the start file and have everything set up automatically. However, in some rare cases, macOS users may need to run the following command first::

Copy

    xcode-select --install

chevron-rightOptional: Running Cyberdrop-DL Script with Custom Parameters[hashtag](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/getting-started/cyberdrop-dl-install#optional-running-cyberdrop-dl-script-with-custom-parameters)

You can open the start script from the zip in a text editor like notepad. At the top of the file, you will this line:

Copy

    set "COMMANDLINE_ARGS="

`COMMANDLINE_ARGS`: Provide any arguments to pass to Cyberdrop-Dl. For more information, refer to the [CLI Arguments section](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/reference/cli-arguments)

circle-info

You **MUST** put the values _inside_ the double quotes. Ex: `set "COMMANDLINE_ARGS=--disable-cache"`

[hashtag](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/getting-started/cyberdrop-dl-install#manual-install)

Manual Install


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/getting-started/cyberdrop-dl-install#id-1.-using-uv)

1\. Using `uv`

The recommended way to install Cyberdrop-DL is using [`uv`arrow-up-right](https://docs.astral.sh/uv)
.

macOS / Linux

Windows

Once you have `uv`, you can install Cyberdrop-DL using:

### 

[hashtag](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/getting-started/cyberdrop-dl-install#id-2.-manual-python-install)

2\. Manual Python Install

If you do not want to or can't use `uv`, you will need to install a compatible python version manually.

If you don't have python, you can find and download it from their official website: [https://www.python.org/downloads/arrow-up-right](https://www.python.org/downloads/)

circle-info

Cyberdrop-DL requires python 3.11, 3.12 or python 3.13. The **RECOMMENDED** version is 3.12+

circle-exclamation

If you are using a version of Cyberdrop-DL from the previous repository (`cyberdrop-dl` instead of `cyberdrop-dl-patched`), you **MUST** uninstall it before installing the patched version.

Once you have python, you can install Cyberdrop-DL directly from pypi using `pipx` or `pip`. In a command prompt/terminal window:

pipx

pip

*   Install `pipx` (if you don't have it already)
    

*   Install cdl
    

circle-exclamation

Using bare `pip` to install `cyberdrop-dl-patched` is discouraged as it may lead to dependency conflicts with global installs and an inconsistent environment. Consider using `uv` or `pipx`

[PreviousGetting Startedchevron-left](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/getting-started)
[NextRunning CDL on Androidchevron-right](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/getting-started/cyberdrop-dl-on-android)

    curl -LsSf https://astral.sh/uv/install.sh | sh

Copy

    powershell -ExecutionPolicy ByPass -c "irm https://astral.sh/uv/install.ps1 | iex"

    uv tool install cyberdrop-dl-patched

    pip uninstall cyberdrop-dl

    pip install pipx

    pip install cyberdrop-dl-patched

# Running CDL on Android | Cyberdrop-DL

Cyberdrop-dl is a terminal app. That means you need a terminal emulator to run it. The defacto choice in Android is [termuxarrow-up-right](https://termux.dev/en/)
.

circle-info

Most of the dependencies need to be compiled from source. A rust compiler is required. This means the installation could take several minutes, especially on low end phones

circle-exclamation

Compiling from source also requires a lot of extra storage. You will need at least 3.4GB just for the installation of CDL

[hashtag](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/getting-started/cyberdrop-dl-on-android#id-1.-install-termux)

1\. Install `termux`


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Termux wiki: [https://wiki.termux.com/wiki/Installationarrow-up-right](https://wiki.termux.com/wiki/Installation)

Install termux from [F-droid (recommended)arrow-up-right](https://f-droid.org/packages/com.termux/)
 or from the [Google Playstore (restricted version)arrow-up-right](https://play.google.com/store/apps/details?id=com.termux)
:

[hashtag](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/getting-started/cyberdrop-dl-on-android#id-2.-install-cyberdrop-dl-patched)

2\. Install `cyberdrop-dl-patched`


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Run the following commands inside termux

Copy

    # Get storage access permission
    termux-setup-storage
    
    # Install dependencies
    pkg upgrade -y
    pkg install rust which micro libjpeg-turbo python uv -y
    
    # Install CDL and setup appdata folder
    uv tool install cyberdrop-dl-patched
    uv tool update-shell
    mkdir /sdcard/cyberdrop-dl
    echo 'alias cyberdrop-dl="cyberdrop-dl --portrait --appdata-folder /sdcard/cyberdrop-dl"' >> ~/.bashrc
    source ~/.bashrc

[hashtag](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/getting-started/cyberdrop-dl-on-android#how-to-update-cyberdrop-dl-patched)

How to update `cyberdrop-dl-patched`?


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Run this command inside termux:

[PreviousCyberdrop-DL Installchevron-left](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/getting-started/cyberdrop-dl-install)
[NextTransition to V8chevron-right](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/upgrade)

Last updated 5 months ago

*   [1\. Install termux](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/getting-started/cyberdrop-dl-on-android#id-1.-install-termux)
    
*   [2\. Install cyberdrop-dl-patched](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/getting-started/cyberdrop-dl-on-android#id-2.-install-cyberdrop-dl-patched)
    
*   [How to update cyberdrop-dl-patched?](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/getting-started/cyberdrop-dl-on-android#how-to-update-cyberdrop-dl-patched)
    

sun-brightdesktopmoon

Copy

    uv tool upgrade cyberdrop-dl-patched

# Frequently Asked Questions | Cyberdrop-DL

[hashtag](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/frequently-asked-questions#what-does-this-do)

What does this do?


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

This is a bulk downloader for the supported sites. It supports resumable downloading (you can close and reopen the program at any time and it will pick up where it left off), and keeps track of your download history to avoid downloading files you've already downloaded in the past.

[hashtag](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/frequently-asked-questions#how-do-i-update-this)

How do I update this?


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

If you are using one of the provided start files, it should do so automatically. Keep in mind that they will only update to the newest version within the same major version. ex: if you are using v8 start scripts, they will update to the latest v8 release. When v9 is out, you will need to download the new start scripts

[hashtag](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/frequently-asked-questions#why-do-i-get-ddos-guard-error-downloading-from-x-site)

Why do i get `DDoS-Guard` error downloading from `x` site?


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

You may need to import cookies. Follow the instructions here: [How to extract cookies (DDoSGuard or login errors) #839arrow-up-right](https://github.com/jbsparrow/CyberDropDownloader/discussions/839)

[hashtag](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/frequently-asked-questions#im-trying-to-report-a-bug-and-they-ask-me-for-a-logs-file.-where-is-this-file)

I'm trying to report a bug and they ask me for a logs file. Where is this file?


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

By default, it'll be in `./AppData/configs/<config>/logs/`

The `AppData` folder is created inside the folder where you run cyberdrop-dl from

[hashtag](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/frequently-asked-questions#what-does-scrape_failures-and-download_failures-mean)

What does `SCRAPE_FAILURES` and `DOWNLOAD_FAILURES` mean?


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Quite simply, almost all of them you see will be HTTP Status codes. Such as: 404 - Not Found (dead link)

You check [this page to learn about what each error code meansarrow-up-right](https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/HTTP/Status)
.

circle-info

Any "Unknown" error, is usually coding related, or it'll be something like the program not being able to find a file extension for a file. You can report unknown error on the issue tracker: [https://github.com/jbsparrow/CyberDropDownloader/issuesarrow-up-right](https://github.com/jbsparrow/CyberDropDownloader/issues)

[hashtag](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/frequently-asked-questions#why-are-all-the-files-skipped)

Why are all the files skipped?


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The program tracks your download history and will skip any files you've previously downloaded to avoid duplicates. You can disable this behavior by using the `--ignore-history` CLI argument or setting `ignore_history` to `true` in the config

[hashtag](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/frequently-asked-questions#the-screen-is-flickering)

The screen is flickering?


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

This issue is likely related to the limitations of the traditional command prompt, which has remained largely unchanged over time. For Windows 10 users, it's recommended to install and use [Windows Terminalarrow-up-right](https://aka.ms/terminal)
 to run Cyberdrop-DL. Windows Terminal is the default on Windows 11.

[hashtag](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/frequently-asked-questions#cyberdrop-dl-is-not-a-recognized-internal-command)

`cyberdrop-dl` is not a recognized internal command


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

This issue is caused by an improper installation of Python, specifically Python not being added to the system PATH.

It is recommended to revisit the [Getting Started](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/getting-started)
 guide and follow the steps provided to reinstall or use one of the latest start scripts

[hashtag](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/frequently-asked-questions#how-do-i-scrape-forum-threads)

How do I scrape forum threads?


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

You need to import cookies to use as authentication for those sites. Follow the instructions here: [How to extract cookies (DDoSGuard or login errors) #839arrow-up-right](https://github.com/jbsparrow/CyberDropDownloader/discussions/839)

[hashtag](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/frequently-asked-questions#why-are-the-filenames-the-way-they-are)

Why are the filenames the way they are?


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Filenames are taken directly from the source website. Blame whoever uploaded it.

[hashtag](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/frequently-asked-questions#how-do-i-fix-ssl-certificate_verify_failed)

How do I fix `[SSL: CERTIFICATE_VERIFY_FAILED]`?


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

This should only appear on macOS, so these instructions are for mac users.

Go to your applications folder, find the python folder inside of it. Run the `Install Certificates` file in that folder.

Go back to where you are running Cyberdrop-DL and delete the `venv` folder if one exists (if not, don't worry). Then try running the program again.

[hashtag](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/frequently-asked-questions#a-thread-site-i-follow-has-new-posts-but-cyberdrop-dl-is-not-detecting-downloading-them-why)

A thread/site i follow has new posts but `cyberdrop-dl` is not detecting / downloading them, why?


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

`cyberdrop-dl` caches requests to made to sites to speed up re-runs and minimize load on those sites. By default, forums are cached for 30 days and any other site is cached for 7 days.

You can run with `--disable-cache` to temporarily disable the cache (CLI only) or change the default values to 0.

See:

[\--forum-cache-expire-afterarrow-up-right](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/reference/configuration-options/global-settings/rate-limiting-options#forum_cache_expire_after)

[\--file-host-cache-expire-afterarrow-up-right](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/reference/configuration-options/global-settings/rate-limiting-options#file_host_cache_expire_after)

*   [Why are the filenames the way they are?](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/frequently-asked-questions#why-are-the-filenames-the-way-they-are)

*   [A thread/site i follow has new posts but cyberdrop-dl is not detecting / downloading them, why?](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/frequently-asked-questions#a-thread-site-i-follow-has-new-posts-but-cyberdrop-dl-is-not-detecting-downloading-them-why)

# Migration to Cyberdrop-DL-Patched | Cyberdrop-DL

If you used the original version of the package (`cyberdrop-dl` instead of `cyberdrop-dl-patched`), you can follow the steps below to migrate.

circle-exclamation

You may need to adjust your config to make sure it's compatible with the newer versions.

See: [Transition to V8arrow-up-right](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/upgrade)

[hashtag](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/migration-to-cyberdrop-dl-patched#if-you-installed-on-your-own-using-pip)

If you installed on your own using pip


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

You can simply uninstall the old version and install the new one using the following commands:

Copy

    pip uninstall -y cyberdrop-dl
    pip install cyberdrop-dl-patched

The command to use the new version will be `cyberdrop-dl-patched`.

[hashtag](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/migration-to-cyberdrop-dl-patched#if-you-installed-using-the-start-files)

If you installed using the start files


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

You can find the new ones here: [new start scriptsarrow-up-right](https://github.com/jbsparrow/CyberDropDownloader/releases/latest)

Put the new start scripts on the same folder as the old ones, them delete the old ones.

You also have to delete any `venv` or `.venv` folder (if you have any)

[NextSimpCity Support Droppedchevron-right](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/simpcity-support-dropped)

# SimpCity Support Dropped | Cyberdrop-DL

[hashtag](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/simpcity-support-dropped#removal-of-simpcity-scraping-support)

Removal of SimpCity Scraping Support


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Support for scraping SimpCity has been removed temporarily. This may be disappointing to some users, but the explanation provided should clarify the reasoning behind this decision. Following the recent DDOS attacks, SimpCity has implemented the following security measures to protect their website:

*   SimpCity has implemented a DDOS-Guard browser check.
    
*   Access is now restricted to [whitelisted email domainsarrow-up-right](https://simpcity.su/threads/emails-august-2024.365869/)
    .
    
*   [New rate limitsarrow-up-right](https://simpcity.su/threads/rate-limit-429-error.397746/)
     have been introduced to protect the site.
    

[hashtag](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/simpcity-support-dropped#why-scraping-simpcity-has-been-disabled)

Why Scraping SimpCity Has Been Disabled


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Cyberdrop-DL allows users to scrape a model’s entire thread quickly, downloading large amounts of content. While convenient, this has created several issues:

*   Large-scale scraping can result in downloading content you may never view.
    
*   Such scraping puts additional load on their servers, particularly during DDOS attacks.
    
*   Scraping provides no direct benefit to SimpCity, and in light of these attacks, they have chosen not to support automated scraping.
    

For these reasons, SimpCity has removed the Cyberdrop-DL thread, and scraping for their site has been disabled in order to reduce the strain on their servers.

[hashtag](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/simpcity-support-dropped#how-to-reduce-the-impact-of-cyberdrop-dl-usage)

How to Reduce the Impact of Cyberdrop-DL Usage


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

To help reduce the load on other websites, the `update_last_forum_post` setting has been enabled by default in all users' configs. This setting speeds up scrapes by picking up where the last session left off, rather than re-scraping entire threads.

You can disable this setting if you prefer, but it is strongly discouraged.

In addition, the default rate-limiting settings have been adjusted to further reduce the impact on websites.

[hashtag](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/simpcity-support-dropped#usage-best-practices)

Usage Best Practices


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

I encourage you to use the program responsibly. Here are some tips to help minimize the impact on websites:

*   Avoid running multiple scraping sessions repeatedly in a short span of time.
    
*   Regularly clean up your URLs file by removing links you no longer need, and reducing how often you run the program.
    
*   Be selective with what you download. It’s helpful to quickly scan content to avoid downloading files you'll delete later.
    

[hashtag](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/simpcity-support-dropped#alternatives-to-scraping-simpcity)

Alternatives to Scraping SimpCity


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

If you wish to continue downloading from SimpCity, you can use Tampermonkey scripts like these ones:

*   [SimpCity Tampermonkey Forum Downloaderarrow-up-right](https://simpcity.su/threads/forum-post-downloader-tampermonkey-script.96714/)
    .
    
*   [Forums Link Grabberarrow-up-right](https://github.com/Garcarius/forumslinkgraber)
    

[PreviousMigration to Cyberdrop-DL-Patchedchevron-left](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/migration-to-cyberdrop-dl-patched)
[NextSupported Websiteschevron-right](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/reference/supported-websites)

Last updated 5 months ago

*   [Removal of SimpCity Scraping Support](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/simpcity-support-dropped#removal-of-simpcity-scraping-support)
    
*   [Why Scraping SimpCity Has Been Disabled](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/simpcity-support-dropped#why-scraping-simpcity-has-been-disabled)
    
*   [How to Reduce the Impact of Cyberdrop-DL Usage](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/simpcity-support-dropped#how-to-reduce-the-impact-of-cyberdrop-dl-usage)
    
*   [Usage Best Practices](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/simpcity-support-dropped#usage-best-practices)

# Transition to V8 | Cyberdrop-DL

triangle-exclamation

V6 introduced some breaking changes: Using a more strict config validation logic, replacing `md5` with `xxh128` as the default hashing algorithm, using a new database schema, among others.

It's recommended to do a manual backup of your current `AppData` folder. You won't be able to rollback to a previous version after the transfer is completed.

You can learn more about these changes on the [release announcementarrow-up-right](https://github.com/jbsparrow/CyberDropDownloader/blob/master/CHANGELOG.md#600---2024-12-23)

circle-exclamation

Even after a successful configuration migration, the program may not start if some values from the previous version’s config are no longer valid. Please follow the on-screen instructions to resolve the issue.

You can use the [Config Options page](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/reference/configuration-options)
 as reference for valid config values

[hashtag](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/upgrade#import-v5-v6-or-v7-config-into-v8)

Import V5, V6 or v7 config into v8


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Good news! If you have a v5-v7 config, CDL can import it. The program will automatically detect the config in the current folder and handle the migration process for you.

All you have to do is replace your old start script (for Windows, that's the `.bat` file) with the v8 start script.

Please note that after the migration is complete, you may still need to manually adjust some values in the config.

If you are migrating from v5 and the migration fails, the database will be rolled back to its previous state. An automatic backup is also made before the migration begins. However, keep in mind that the backup only includes the database, not the config files.

circle-info

Support for v5 and v6 (config, database and auto-migration) is deprecated and will be removed in v9

[hashtag](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/upgrade#import-v4-config)

Import V4 config


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

circle-exclamation

V4 import is no longer supported. Last version with v4 support was `6.5.0`. To upgrade to the latest version, you need to perform a sequential upgrade. First, update CDL to `6.5.0`, import your v4 files, and then update to the latest version.

You can install `6.5.0` with pip by running:

Copy

    pip install cyberdrop-dl-patched==6.5.0

Built into Cyberdrop-DL is a tool that allows you to import both your configs and your history DB from a v4 version of Cyberdrop-DL. You can use it by selecting "Import V4 Items".

### 

[hashtag](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/upgrade#import-your-v4-configs)

Import Your V4 Configs

The config files will be located in the folder that you were previously running Cyberdrop-DL in. Start CDL, choose the option `Import v4 config` and follow the on screen instructions

circle-info

If you weren't using the config previously, you don't need to import it.

However, if you were primarily using CLI Arguments with V4, some of the arguments has been replaced.

If you don't end up using the import feature, make sure you also change the default config in the program if that's something you want to do.

### 

[hashtag](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/upgrade#import-your-v4-database)

Import Your V4 Database

For a lot of people, the `download_history.sqlite` file will be in the same folder as your start file (or wherever you are running Cyberdrop-DL).

If it's not there, you can find it here:

Windows:

macOS:

Linux:

To import it, start CDL, choose the option `Import v4 database` and follow the on screen instructions

circle-info

The old `download_history.sqlite` file is no longer used by Cyberdrop-DL. After you import it, you can delete the old one.

If you don't want to import previous download history, you can just delete it.

[PreviousRunning CDL on Androidchevron-left](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/getting-started/cyberdrop-dl-on-android)
[NextFrequently Asked Questionschevron-right](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/frequently-asked-questions)

Default

# Special Type Options | Cyberdrop-DL

[hashtag](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/reference/configuration-options/special_setting_types#additiveargs)

`AdditiveArgs`


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Special type for some settings that accept multiple values as input (`lists` or `sets`). When passing values as CLI arguments, if the first value is `+`, any value after it will be added to the values specified in the config file instead of overriding it. Similarly, if the first value is `-`, any value after it will be removed from the values specified in the config

### 

[hashtag](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/reference/configuration-options/special_setting_types#examples)

Examples

If you have the following `skip_hosts` setting in you config file:

Copy

    skip_hosts:
      - drive.google.com
      - youtube.com
      - facebook.com

You will get the following results:

Value you used

Value CDL interpreted

Details

`--skip-hosts instagram.com`

`[instagram.com]`

config values were overridden by CLI values

`--skip-hosts "+" instagram.com`

`[drive.google.com, youtube.com, facebook.com, instagram.com]`

config values and CLI values were merged

`--skip-hosts "-" drive.google.com youtube.com`

`[facebook.com]`

CLI values were removed from the config values

circle-info

Always use quotes for "+" and "-" to make sure your shell does not try to parse them as additional flags

[hashtag](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/reference/configuration-options/special_setting_types#boolflag)

`BoolFlag`


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

A special kind of `bool`. Within a config file, it can have a `true` or `false` value. However, when used via CLI, the value is assumed from the flag name. The normal name is `true`, and prefixing the name with `--no` means `false`.

### 

[hashtag](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/reference/configuration-options/special_setting_types#examples-1)

Examples

Value you used

Value CDL interpreted

`--auto-dedupe`

auto-dedupe: `true`

`--no-auto-dedupe`

auto-dedupe: `false`

[hashtag](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/reference/configuration-options/special_setting_types#bytesize)

`ByteSize`


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

A special kind of `int` that also accepts suffixes like `GB`, `MiB` and `KB` to specify valid values

In conformance with IEC 80000-13 Standard, `1KB` means `1000 bytes`, and `1KiB` means `1024 bytes`. In general, including a middle 'i' will cause the unit to be interpreted as a power of 2, rather than a power of 10.

### 

[hashtag](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/reference/configuration-options/special_setting_types#examples-2)

Examples

Value you used

Value CDL interpreted

`1GB`

`1.000.000.000 bytes`

`512`

`512 bytes`

`1MiB`

`1.048.576 bytes`

circle-info

`ByteSize` is also used for some settings to specify speed and it's interpreted as `<value> / second`. ex: `8MB` means `8MB/s`

[PreviousConfiguration Optionschevron-left](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/reference/configuration-options)
[NextAuthenticationchevron-right](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/reference/configuration-options/authentication)

Last updated 5 months ago

*   [AdditiveArgs](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/reference/configuration-options/special_setting_types#additiveargs)
    
*   [Examples](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/reference/configuration-options/special_setting_types#examples)
    
*   [BoolFlag](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/reference/configuration-options/special_setting_types#boolflag)
    
*   [Examples](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/reference/configuration-options/special_setting_types#examples-1)
    
*   [ByteSize](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/reference/configuration-options/special_setting_types#bytesize)
    
*   [Examples](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/reference/configuration-options/special_setting_types#examples-2)

# Configuration Options | Cyberdrop-DL

There are three type of config files: config settings, global settings and authentication settings.

[user-lockAuthenticationchevron-right](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/reference/configuration-options/authentication)
[earth-americasGlobal Settingschevron-right](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/reference/configuration-options/global-settings)
[screwdriver-wrenchSettingschevron-right](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/reference/configuration-options/settings)

circle-info

**Global Settings** and **Authentication Settings** are "global". They apply to _all_ config settings. You can set them once and never touch them again.

Each config setting will be setup by default to have a separate `URLs.txt` files and separate log files.

# File Size Limits | Cyberdrop-DL

All options on this category take a `ByteSize` input ([more info here](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/reference/configuration-options/special_setting_types#bytesize)
).

Type

Default

`ByteSize`

`0`

Setting any of these options to `0` means that limit is `disabled`

*   `maximum_image_filesize`
    
*   `minimum_image_filesize`
    
*   `maximum_video_filesize`
    
*   `minimum_video_filesize`
    
*   `maximum_other_filesize`
    
*   `minimum_other_filesize`

# Welcome! | Cyberdrop-DL Development Docs | Cyberdrop-DL

Cyberdrop-DL is an open source asynchronous downloader maintained by [jbsparrowarrow-up-right](https://github.com/jbsparrow)
. It's goal is to act as a bulk downloader for various sites you will find around the web.

[globe-pointerSupported Websiteschevron-right](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/dev/reference/supported-websites)

[hashtag](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/dev#want-to-jump-right-in)

Want to jump right in?


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Explore the Getting Started guide to quickly familiarize yourself with the setup process and get started with the software.

[bullseye-arrowGetting Startedchevron-right](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/dev/getting-started)

# Dupe Cleanup Options | Cyberdrop-DL

Cyberdrop-DL maintains an internal database of all downloaded files, indexed by their hashes. This can be used to automatically delete newly downloaded files if they were downloaded before. To enable auto dupe cleanup:

1.  Set `hashing` to `IN_PLACE` or `POST_DOWNLOAD`
    
2.  Set `auto_dedupe` to `true`
    

[hashtag](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/reference/configuration-options/settings/dupe_cleanup_options#add_md5_hash)

`add_md5_hash`


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Type

Default

`bool`

`false`

If enabled, calculates the `md5` hash for every downloaded file and store it in the internal database. This allows the program to match files with sites that provide hash information before downloading them, skipping the download altogether if a match is found

circle-info

`md5` was the default hashing algorithm of Cyberdrop-DL V5. Since v6, the default algorithm is `xxhash128`.

[hashtag](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/reference/configuration-options/settings/dupe_cleanup_options#add_sha256_hash)

`add_sha256_hash`


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Type

Default

`bool`

`false`

If enabled, calculates the `sha256` hash for every downloaded file and store it in the internal database. This allows the program to match files with sites that provide hash information before downloading them, skipping the download altogether if a match is found

[hashtag](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/reference/configuration-options/settings/dupe_cleanup_options#auto_dedupe)

`auto_dedupe`


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Type

Default

`bool`

`false`

Enables deduping files functionality. Needs `hashing` to be enabled

The `auto_dedupe` feature scans the database for files with matching hashes and sizes, automatically deleting any duplicates and retaining only the oldest copy.

Deletion will only occur if two or more matching files are found during the database search.

circle-exclamation

Auto dedupe will delete files if you have _ever_ downloaded them before, even if you no longer have the original download on disk

[hashtag](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/reference/configuration-options/settings/dupe_cleanup_options#hashing)

`hashing`


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Type

Default

Restrictions

`HASHING`

`OFF`

Must be `OFF`, `IN_PLACE` or `POST_DOWNLOAD`

There are three possible options for hashing:

1.  `OFF`: disables hashing
    
2.  `IN_PLACE`: performs hashing after each download
    
3.  `POST_DOWNLOAD`: performs hashing after all downloads have completed
    

The default hashing algorithm is `xxh128`. You can enable additional hashing algorithms, but you can not replace the default.

[hashtag](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/reference/configuration-options/settings/dupe_cleanup_options#send_deleted_to_trash)

`send_deleted_to_trash`


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Type

Default

`bool`

`false`

Deduped files are sent to the trash bin instead of being deleted

[PreviousDownload Optionschevron-left](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/reference/configuration-options/settings/download_options)
[NextFile Size Limitschevron-right](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/reference/configuration-options/settings/file_size_limits)

Last updated 5 months ago

*   [add\_md5\_hash](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/reference/configuration-options/settings/dupe_cleanup_options#add_md5_hash)
    
*   [add\_sha256\_hash](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/reference/configuration-options/settings/dupe_cleanup_options#add_sha256_hash)
    
*   [auto\_dedupe](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/reference/configuration-options/settings/dupe_cleanup_options#auto_dedupe)
    
*   [hashing](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/reference/configuration-options/settings/dupe_cleanup_options#hashing)
    
*   [send\_deleted\_to\_trash](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/reference/configuration-options/settings/dupe_cleanup_options#send_deleted_to_trash)

# Browser Cookies | Cyberdrop-DL

Cyberdrop-DL can extract cookies from your browser. These can be used for websites that require login or to pass DDoS-Guard challenges. Only cookies from supported websites are extracted

circle-exclamation

The `user-agent` config value **MUST** match the `user-agent` of the browser from which you imported the cookies. If they do not match, the cookies will not work

[hashtag](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/reference/configuration-options/settings/browser_cookies#auto_import)

`auto_import`


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Type

Default

`bool`

`false`

Toggles automatic import of cookies at the start of each run

[hashtag](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/reference/configuration-options/settings/browser_cookies#browser)

`browser`


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Type

Default

`BROWSER`

`firefox`

A browser to use for extraction. Browser must be a supported browser's name.

### 

[hashtag](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/reference/configuration-options/settings/browser_cookies#supported-browsers)

[hashtag](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/reference/configuration-options/settings/browser_cookies#sites)

`sites`


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Type

Default

`list[DOMAINS]`

`[<<ALL_SUPPORTED_SITES>>]`

List of domains to extract cookies from. You can put any domain on the list, even if they are not officially supported.

[hashtag](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/reference/configuration-options/settings/browser_cookies#manual-cookie-extraction)

Manual Cookie Extraction


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

If cookie extraction fails, you can manually extract the cookies from your browser using tools like [cookie-editorarrow-up-right](https://cookie-editor.com/)
 and save them at `AppData/Cookies/<site_name>.txt`. The file must be a Netscape formatted cookie file. You can use any name for the file as long as it has a `.txt` extension.

See: [How to extract cookies (DDoSGuard or login errors) #839arrow-up-right](https://github.com/jbsparrow/CyberDropDownloader/discussions/839)
 for detailed instructions

circle-info

Multiple cookie files are supported. You could have a `SocialMediaGirls.txt` file and a `cyberdrop.txt` file, for example

[PreviousSettingschevron-left](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/reference/configuration-options/settings)
[NextDownload Optionschevron-right](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/reference/configuration-options/settings/download_options)

# Getting Started | Cyberdrop-DL Development Docs | Cyberdrop-DL

[hashtag](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/dev/getting-started#installing-cyberdrop-dl)

Installing Cyberdrop-DL


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

There are two ways to install Cyberdrop-DL. The first is the easy method, where you simply download the start scripts. The start scripts will automatically install a compatible python version and then install Cyberdrop-DL.

The second method is installing cyberdrop-dl directly from pypi using `uv`, `pipx` or `pip`

For instructions, see:

[downloadCyberdrop-DL Installchevron-right](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/dev/getting-started/cyberdrop-dl-install)
[androidRunning CDL on Androidchevron-right](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/dev/getting-started/cyberdrop-dl-on-android)

[hashtag](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/dev/getting-started#what-now)

What now?


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

If you downloaded the start scripts, just open the start script with the name of the OS you are using. For a manual install, execute the program with this command:

Copy

    cyberdrop-dl-patched

On the main screen, you can use the 'Edit URLs' option to add the URLs for the files you wish to download, them select the `download` option. That's it!

However, Cyberdrop-DL has a ton of configuration options if you want more control over the downloads. You may want to review the following:

[slidersConfiguration Optionschevron-right](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/dev/reference/configuration-options)
[rectangle-terminalCLI Argumentschevron-right](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/dev/reference/cli-arguments)
[envelope-open-textNotificationschevron-right](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/dev/reference/notifications)

By default, all config files are under the `AppData` folder, which is created on the same directory that CDL it run from.

You may also want to peek at what websites the program actually supports:

[globe-pointerSupported Websiteschevron-right](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/dev/reference/supported-websites)

If you have any issues, perhaps the [FAQ](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/dev/frequently-asked-questions)
 might help you!

[PreviousWelcome!chevron-left](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/dev)
[NextCyberdrop-DL Installchevron-right](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/dev/getting-started/cyberdrop-dl-install)

Last updated 5 months ago

sun-brightdesktopmoon

sun-brightdesktopmoon

# Notifications | Cyberdrop-DL

Cyberdrop-DL generates a report at the end of a run with stats about all the downloads, total runtime, errors, deduplication report, etc. By default, this report is only shown in the console and at the end of the main log file.

You can set up CDL to sent you the report via discord, email, a native notification of your OS, telegram and many other services.

[hashtag](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/reference/notifications#notifications-via-discord)

Notifications via Discord


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

To get notifications via discord, you need to provide a discord `webhook_url` inside the `setting.yaml` of the config you are running.

You can learn how to setup a webhook following the [official discord guidearrow-up-right](https://support.discord.com/hc/en-us/articles/228383668-Intro-to-Webhooks)
.

Optionally, you can add the tag `attach_logs=` as a prefix to your webhook url. This will tell CDL to include a copy of the main log as an attachment to Discord.

[hashtag](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/reference/notifications#notifications-to-other-services-via-apprise)

Notifications to other services (via Apprise)


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Cyberdrop-DL uses [Apprisearrow-up-right](https://github.com/caronc/apprise)
 to send notifications to any of the services than they support.

### 

[hashtag](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/reference/notifications#how-to-setup-apprise)

How to setup Apprise

To send notifications via Apprise, you need to create an `apprise.txt` file inside `AppData/Configs/<config_name>`, where `<config_name>` if the config you want to use. The file must contain a list of URLs and they must be in the format of one of the supported apprise services.

You can check the full list of supported services [herearrow-up-right](https://github.com/caronc/apprise/wiki)
 and the URL format than each one uses [herearrow-up-right](https://github.com/caronc/apprise?tab=readme-ov-file#supported-notifications)
.

Apprise services also support the `attach_logs=` tag to send the main log as an attachment.

### 

[hashtag](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/reference/notifications#troubleshooting-apprise-notifications)

Troubleshooting Apprise notifications

Cyberdrop-DL will show you a message at the end of a run telling you if the apprise notifications were successfully sent or not. If you are having trouble getting notifications via Apprise, follow their [troubleshooting guidearrow-up-right](https://github.com/caronc/apprise/wiki/Troubleshooting)
.

circle-info

When running on Windows, Cyberdrop-DL will setup OS notifications by default.

You can disable them by deleting the `windows://` line from the default `apprise.txt` file. You can also completely delete the file if you don't have any other notification setup.

[hashtag](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/reference/notifications#examples)

Examples


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Email

Email + Logs

Native OS notifications

Discord + Logs

To get notifications via email, use this URL format in your `apprise.txt` file:

Add `attach_logs` to your email URL in your `apprise.txt` file:

Some operating systems require additional dependencies for notifications to work. Cyberdrop-DL includes the required dependencies for Windows. Follow the url on the OS name to get additional information on how to set them up.

OS

Syntax

[Linux (DBus Notifications)arrow-up-right](https://github.com/caronc/apprise/wiki/Notify_dbus)

`dbus://` `qt://` `glib://` `kde://`

[Linux (Gnome Notifications)arrow-up-right](https://github.com/caronc/apprise/wiki/Notify_gnome)

`gnome://`

[macOSarrow-up-right](https://github.com/caronc/apprise/wiki/Notify_macosx)

`macosx://`

[Windowsarrow-up-right](https://github.com/caronc/apprise/wiki/Notify_windows)

`windows://`

Add `attach_logs` to the `webhook_url` config option:

[PreviousCLI Argumentschevron-left](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/reference/cli-arguments)

# Files | Cyberdrop-DL

[hashtag](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/reference/configuration-options/settings/files#download_folder)

`download_folder`


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Type

Default

`Path`

`Downloads`

The path to the folder you want Cyberdrop-DL to download files to.

[hashtag](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/reference/configuration-options/settings/files#dump_json)

`dump_json`


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Type

Default

`bool`

`False`

If enabled, CDL will created a [json linesarrow-up-right](https://jsonlines.org/)
 files with the information about every file downloaded in the current run. The path to this file will be the same as `--main-log` but with the extension `.results.jsonl`

Each line in the file will contain the following details (this may change on future versions):

Copy

    {
        "url": "https://store9.gofile.io/download/web/7c88c147-ABCD-4e4d-9a6c-12345678/a_video.mp4",
        "referer": "https://gofile.io/d/ABC123",
        "download_folder": "Downloads/Cyberdrop-DL Downloads/test_album (GoFile)",
        "filename": "0hxte0li0o931lwgcrzbz_source.mp4",
        "original_filename": "a_video.mp4",
        "download_filename": "0hxte0li0o931lwgcrzbz_source.mp4",
        "filesize": 12054723,
        "ext": ".mp4",
        "debrid_link": null,
        "duration": null,
        "album_id": "ABC123",
        "datetime": "2025-01-22T11:00:07",
        "parents": ["https://a_forum.com/threads/<name>.54321/post-123123"],
        "parent_threads": ["https://a_forum.com/threads/<name>.54321"],
        "partial_file": "Downloads/Cyberdrop-DL Downloads/test_album (GoFile)/a_video.mp4.part",
        "complete_file": "Downloads/Cyberdrop-DL Downloads/test_album (GoFile)/a_video.mp4",
        "hash": "xxh128:53ee56b7bfafa31b8780a572e9783df3",
        "downloaded": true,
        "attempts": 1
    
    }

[hashtag](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/reference/configuration-options/settings/files#input_file)

`input_file`


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Type

Default

`Path`

`AppData/Configs/{config}/URLs.txt`

The path to the text file containing the URLs you want to download. Each line should be a single URL.

You can also use `html` code. Cyberdrop-DL will parse all the links on the HTML

[hashtag](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/reference/configuration-options/settings/files#save_pages_html)

`save_pages_html`


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Type

Default

`bool`

`False`

CDL will save to disk a copy of every requests as an html file. The files will be saved to a folder named `cdl_responses`, located in the same folder as the main log file.

circle-info

Not every request made by CDL returns an HTML page (ex: API requests generally return JSON data). Only HTML responses will be saved

[PreviousFile Size Limitschevron-left](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/reference/configuration-options/settings/file_size_limits)
[NextIgnore Optionschevron-right](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/reference/configuration-options/settings/ignore_options)

# SimpCity Support Dropped | Cyberdrop-DL Development Docs | Cyberdrop-DL

[hashtag](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/dev/simpcity-support-dropped#removal-of-simpcity-scraping-support)

Removal of SimpCity Scraping Support


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Support for scraping SimpCity has been removed temporarily. This may be disappointing to some users, but the explanation provided should clarify the reasoning behind this decision. Following the recent DDOS attacks, SimpCity has implemented the following security measures to protect their website:

*   SimpCity has implemented a DDOS-Guard browser check.
    
*   Access is now restricted to [whitelisted email domainsarrow-up-right](https://simpcity.su/threads/emails-august-2024.365869/)
    .
    
*   [New rate limitsarrow-up-right](https://simpcity.su/threads/rate-limit-429-error.397746/)
     have been introduced to protect the site.
    

[hashtag](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/dev/simpcity-support-dropped#why-scraping-simpcity-has-been-disabled)

Why Scraping SimpCity Has Been Disabled


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Cyberdrop-DL allows users to scrape a model’s entire thread quickly, downloading large amounts of content. While convenient, this has created several issues:

*   Large-scale scraping can result in downloading content you may never view.
    
*   Such scraping puts additional load on their servers, particularly during DDOS attacks.
    
*   Scraping provides no direct benefit to SimpCity, and in light of these attacks, they have chosen not to support automated scraping.
    

For these reasons, SimpCity has removed the Cyberdrop-DL thread, and scraping for their site has been disabled in order to reduce the strain on their servers.

[hashtag](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/dev/simpcity-support-dropped#how-to-reduce-the-impact-of-cyberdrop-dl-usage)

How to Reduce the Impact of Cyberdrop-DL Usage


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

To help reduce the load on other websites, the `update_last_forum_post` setting has been enabled by default in all users' configs. This setting speeds up scrapes by picking up where the last session left off, rather than re-scraping entire threads.

You can disable this setting if you prefer, but it is strongly discouraged.

In addition, the default rate-limiting settings have been adjusted to further reduce the impact on websites.

[hashtag](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/dev/simpcity-support-dropped#usage-best-practices)

Usage Best Practices


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

I encourage you to use the program responsibly. Here are some tips to help minimize the impact on websites:

*   Avoid running multiple scraping sessions repeatedly in a short span of time.
    
*   Regularly clean up your URLs file by removing links you no longer need, and reducing how often you run the program.
    
*   Be selective with what you download. It’s helpful to quickly scan content to avoid downloading files you'll delete later.
    

[hashtag](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/dev/simpcity-support-dropped#alternatives-to-scraping-simpcity)

Alternatives to Scraping SimpCity


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

If you wish to continue downloading from SimpCity, you can use Tampermonkey scripts like these ones:

*   [SimpCity Tampermonkey Forum Downloaderarrow-up-right](https://simpcity.su/threads/forum-post-downloader-tampermonkey-script.96714/)
    .
    
*   [Forums Link Grabberarrow-up-right](https://github.com/Garcarius/forumslinkgraber)
    

[PreviousMigration to Cyberdrop-DL-Patchedchevron-left](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/dev/migration-to-cyberdrop-dl-patched)
[NextSupported Websiteschevron-right](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/dev/reference/supported-websites)

Last updated 5 months ago

*   [Removal of SimpCity Scraping Support](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/dev/simpcity-support-dropped#removal-of-simpcity-scraping-support)
    
*   [Why Scraping SimpCity Has Been Disabled](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/dev/simpcity-support-dropped#why-scraping-simpcity-has-been-disabled)
    
*   [How to Reduce the Impact of Cyberdrop-DL Usage](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/dev/simpcity-support-dropped#how-to-reduce-the-impact-of-cyberdrop-dl-usage)
    
*   [Usage Best Practices](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/dev/simpcity-support-dropped#usage-best-practices)
    
*   [Alternatives to Scraping SimpCity](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/dev/simpcity-support-dropped#alternatives-to-scraping-simpcity)

# Ignore Options | Cyberdrop-DL

[hashtag](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/reference/configuration-options/settings/ignore_options#exclude_audio)

`exclude_audio`


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Type

Default

`bool`

`false`

When this is set to `true`, the program will skip downloading audio files.

[hashtag](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/reference/configuration-options/settings/ignore_options#exclude_images)

`exclude_images`


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Type

Default

`bool`

`false`

When this is set to `true`, the program will skip downloading image files.

[hashtag](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/reference/configuration-options/settings/ignore_options#exclude_videos)

`exclude_videos`


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Type

Default

`bool`

`false`

When this is set to `true`, the program will skip downloading video files.

[hashtag](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/reference/configuration-options/settings/ignore_options#exclude_other)

`exclude_other`


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Type

Default

`bool`

`false`

When this is set to `true`, the program will skip downloading non media files files.

[hashtag](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/reference/configuration-options/settings/ignore_options#exclude_files_with_no_extension)

`exclude_files_with_no_extension`


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Type

Default

`bool`

`true`

When this is set to `true`, the program will skip downloading files without an extension.

circle-info

CDL internally assumes any file without an extension is an `.mp4` file. That means any option that applies to videos like `--exclude-videos` and `--minimum-video-size` will apply to them. The actual file will still be downloaded without an extension

[hashtag](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/reference/configuration-options/settings/ignore_options#filename_regex_filter)

`filename_regex_filter`


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Type

Default

`NonEmptyStr` or `null`

`null`

Any download with a filename that matches this regex expression will be skipped

[hashtag](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/reference/configuration-options/settings/ignore_options#ignore_coomer_ads)

`ignore_coomer_ads`


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Type

Default

`bool`

`false`

When this is set to `true`, CDL will skip posts marked as `#ad` by models.

Despite the name, this option affects all kemono based sites (Nekohouse, Kemono and Coomer)

circle-info

This requires fetching all posts with the tag `#ad` first and them filter them out from the normal ones. This means at least 1 additional request per profile is needed, depending on how many ads the profile has.

[hashtag](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/reference/configuration-options/settings/ignore_options#ignore_coomer_post_content)

`ignore_coomer_post_content`


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Type

Default

`bool`

`true`

When this is set to `false`, CDL will scan the text inside each post for URLs and process them.

Despite the name, this option affects all kemono based sites (Nekohouse, Kemono and Coomer)

circle-exclamation

This requires making 50x more requests when downloading an entire profile. Only enable this option if you actually need it

[hashtag](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/reference/configuration-options/settings/ignore_options#only_hosts)

`only_hosts`


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Type

Default

Additional Info

`list[NonEmptyStr]`

`[]`

This is an [`AdditiveArg`](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/reference/configuration-options/special_setting_types#additiveargs)

You can supply hosts that you'd like the program to exclusively scrape/download from. This setting accepts any domain, even if they are no supported.

[hashtag](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/reference/configuration-options/settings/ignore_options#skip_hosts)

`skip_hosts`


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Type

Default

Additional Info

`list[NonEmptyStr]`

`[]`

This is an [`AdditiveArg`](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/reference/configuration-options/special_setting_types#additiveargs)

You can supply hosts that you'd like the program to skip, to not scrape/download from them. This setting accepts any domain, even if they are no supported.

[hashtag](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/reference/configuration-options/settings/ignore_options#exclude_before)

`exclude_before`


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Type

Default

Additional Info

`date` or `null`

`null`

The date should a valid ISO 8601 format, for example, `2021-12-23`

Do not download files uploaded before this date.

[hashtag](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/reference/configuration-options/settings/ignore_options#exclude_after)

`exclude_after`


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Type

Default

Additional Info

`date` or `null`

`null`

The date should a valid ISO 8601 format, for example, `2021-12-23`

Do not download files uploaded after this date.

# Migration to Cyberdrop-DL-Patched | Cyberdrop-DL Development Docs | Cyberdrop-DL

If you used the original version of the package (`cyberdrop-dl` instead of `cyberdrop-dl-patched`), you can follow the steps below to migrate.

circle-exclamation

You may need to adjust your config to make sure it's compatible with the newer versions.

See: [Transition to V8arrow-up-right](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/upgrade)

[hashtag](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/dev/migration-to-cyberdrop-dl-patched#if-you-installed-on-your-own-using-pip)

If you installed on your own using pip


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

You can simply uninstall the old version and install the new one using the following commands:

Copy

    pip uninstall -y cyberdrop-dl
    pip install cyberdrop-dl-patched

The command to use the new version will be `cyberdrop-dl-patched`.

[hashtag](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/dev/migration-to-cyberdrop-dl-patched#if-you-installed-using-the-start-files)

If you installed using the start files


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

You can find the new ones here: [new start scriptsarrow-up-right](https://github.com/jbsparrow/CyberDropDownloader/releases/latest)

Put the new start scripts on the same folder as the old ones, them delete the old ones.

You also have to delete any `venv` or `.venv` folder (if you have any)

[PreviousFrequently Asked Questionschevron-left](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/dev/frequently-asked-questions)
[NextSimpCity Support Droppedchevron-right](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/dev/simpcity-support-dropped)

Last updated 5 months ago

sun-brightdesktopmoon

sun-brightdesktopmoon

# Transition to V8 | Cyberdrop-DL Development Docs | Cyberdrop-DL

triangle-exclamation

V6 introduced some breaking changes: Using a more strict config validation logic, replacing `md5` with `xxh128` as the default hashing algorithm, using a new database schema, among others.

It's recommended to do a manual backup of your current `AppData` folder. You won't be able to rollback to a previous version after the transfer is completed.

You can learn more about these changes on the [release announcementarrow-up-right](https://github.com/jbsparrow/CyberDropDownloader/blob/master/CHANGELOG.md#600---2024-12-23)

circle-exclamation

Even after a successful configuration migration, the program may not start if some values from the previous version’s config are no longer valid. Please follow the on-screen instructions to resolve the issue.

You can use the [Config Options page](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/dev/reference/configuration-options)
 as reference for valid config values

[hashtag](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/dev/upgrade#import-v5-v6-or-v7-config-into-v8)

Import V5, V6 or v7 config into v8


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Good news! If you have a v5-v7 config, CDL can import it. The program will automatically detect the config in the current folder and handle the migration process for you.

All you have to do is replace your old start script (for Windows, that's the `.bat` file) with the v8 start script.

Please note that after the migration is complete, you may still need to manually adjust some values in the config.

If you are migrating from v5 and the migration fails, the database will be rolled back to its previous state. An automatic backup is also made before the migration begins. However, keep in mind that the backup only includes the database, not the config files.

circle-info

Support for v5 and v6 (config, database and auto-migration) is deprecated and will be removed in v9

[hashtag](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/dev/upgrade#import-v4-config)

Import V4 config


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

circle-exclamation

V4 import is no longer supported. Last version with v4 support was `6.5.0`. To upgrade to the latest version, you need to perform a sequential upgrade. First, update CDL to `6.5.0`, import your v4 files, and then update to the latest version.

You can install `6.5.0` with pip by running:

Copy

    pip install cyberdrop-dl-patched==6.5.0

Built into Cyberdrop-DL is a tool that allows you to import both your configs and your history DB from a v4 version of Cyberdrop-DL. You can use it by selecting "Import V4 Items".

### 

[hashtag](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/dev/upgrade#import-your-v4-configs)

Import Your V4 Configs

The config files will be located in the folder that you were previously running Cyberdrop-DL in. Start CDL, choose the option `Import v4 config` and follow the on screen instructions

circle-info

If you weren't using the config previously, you don't need to import it.

However, if you were primarily using CLI Arguments with V4, some of the arguments has been replaced.

If you don't end up using the import feature, make sure you also change the default config in the program if that's something you want to do.

### 

[hashtag](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/dev/upgrade#import-your-v4-database)

Import Your V4 Database

For a lot of people, the `download_history.sqlite` file will be in the same folder as your start file (or wherever you are running Cyberdrop-DL).

If it's not there, you can find it here:

Windows:

macOS:

Linux:

To import it, start CDL, choose the option `Import v4 database` and follow the on screen instructions

circle-info

The old `download_history.sqlite` file is no longer used by Cyberdrop-DL. After you import it, you can delete the old one.

If you don't want to import previous download history, you can just delete it.

[PreviousRunning CDL on Androidchevron-left](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/dev/getting-started/cyberdrop-dl-on-android)
[NextFrequently Asked Questionschevron-right](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/dev/frequently-asked-questions)

# Running CDL on Android | Cyberdrop-DL Development Docs | Cyberdrop-DL

Cyberdrop-dl is a terminal app. That means you need a terminal emulator to run it. The defacto choice in Android is [termuxarrow-up-right](https://termux.dev/en/)
.

circle-info

Most of the dependencies need to be compiled from source. A rust compiler is required. This means the installation could take several minutes, especially on low end phones

circle-exclamation

Compiling from source also requires a lot of extra storage. You will need at least 3.4GB just for the installation of CDL

[hashtag](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/dev/getting-started/cyberdrop-dl-on-android#id-1.-install-termux)

1\. Install `termux`


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Termux wiki: [https://wiki.termux.com/wiki/Installationarrow-up-right](https://wiki.termux.com/wiki/Installation)

Install termux from [F-droid (recommended)arrow-up-right](https://f-droid.org/packages/com.termux/)
 or from the [Google Playstore (restricted version)arrow-up-right](https://play.google.com/store/apps/details?id=com.termux)
:

[hashtag](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/dev/getting-started/cyberdrop-dl-on-android#id-2.-install-cyberdrop-dl-patched)

2\. Install `cyberdrop-dl-patched`


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Run the following commands inside termux

Copy

    # Get storage access permission
    termux-setup-storage
    
    # Install dependencies
    pkg upgrade -y
    pkg install rust which micro libjpeg-turbo python uv -y
    
    # Install CDL and setup appdata folder
    uv tool install cyberdrop-dl-patched
    uv tool update-shell
    mkdir /sdcard/cyberdrop-dl
    echo 'alias cyberdrop-dl="cyberdrop-dl --portrait --appdata-folder /sdcard/cyberdrop-dl"' >> ~/.bashrc
    source ~/.bashrc

[hashtag](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/dev/getting-started/cyberdrop-dl-on-android#how-to-update-cyberdrop-dl-patched)

How to update `cyberdrop-dl-patched`?


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Run this command inside termux:

[PreviousCyberdrop-DL Installchevron-left](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/dev/getting-started/cyberdrop-dl-install)
[NextTransition to V8chevron-right](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/dev/upgrade)

Last updated 5 months ago

*   [1\. Install termux](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/dev/getting-started/cyberdrop-dl-on-android#id-1.-install-termux)
    
*   [2\. Install cyberdrop-dl-patched](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/dev/getting-started/cyberdrop-dl-on-android#id-2.-install-cyberdrop-dl-patched)
