# Frequently Asked Questions | Cyberdrop-DL Development Docs | Cyberdrop-DL

[hashtag](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/dev/frequently-asked-questions#what-does-this-do)

What does this do?


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

This is a bulk downloader for the supported sites. It supports resumable downloading (you can close and reopen the program at any time and it will pick up where it left off), and keeps track of your download history to avoid downloading files you've already downloaded in the past.

[hashtag](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/dev/frequently-asked-questions#how-do-i-update-this)

How do I update this?


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

If you are using one of the provided start files, it should do so automatically. Keep in mind that they will only update to the newest version within the same major version. ex: if you are using v8 start scripts, they will update to the latest v8 release. When v9 is out, you will need to download the new start scripts

[hashtag](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/dev/frequently-asked-questions#why-do-i-get-ddos-guard-error-downloading-from-x-site)

Why do i get `DDoS-Guard` error downloading from `x` site?


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

You may need to import cookies. Follow the instructions here: [How to extract cookies (DDoSGuard or login errors) #839arrow-up-right](https://github.com/jbsparrow/CyberDropDownloader/discussions/839)

[hashtag](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/dev/frequently-asked-questions#im-trying-to-report-a-bug-and-they-ask-me-for-a-logs-file.-where-is-this-file)

I'm trying to report a bug and they ask me for a logs file. Where is this file?


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

By default, it'll be in `./AppData/configs/<config>/logs/`

The `AppData` folder is created inside the folder where you run cyberdrop-dl from

[hashtag](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/dev/frequently-asked-questions#what-does-scrape_failures-and-download_failures-mean)

What does `SCRAPE_FAILURES` and `DOWNLOAD_FAILURES` mean?


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Quite simply, almost all of them you see will be HTTP Status codes. Such as: 404 - Not Found (dead link)

You check [this page to learn about what each error code meansarrow-up-right](https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/HTTP/Status)
.

circle-info

Any "Unknown" error, is usually coding related, or it'll be something like the program not being able to find a file extension for a file. You can report unknown error on the issue tracker: [https://github.com/jbsparrow/CyberDropDownloader/issuesarrow-up-right](https://github.com/jbsparrow/CyberDropDownloader/issues)

[hashtag](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/dev/frequently-asked-questions#why-are-all-the-files-skipped)

Why are all the files skipped?


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The program tracks your download history and will skip any files you've previously downloaded to avoid duplicates. You can disable this behavior by using the `--ignore-history` CLI argument or setting `ignore_history` to `true` in the config

[hashtag](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/dev/frequently-asked-questions#the-screen-is-flickering)

The screen is flickering?


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

This issue is likely related to the limitations of the traditional command prompt, which has remained largely unchanged over time. For Windows 10 users, it's recommended to install and use [Windows Terminalarrow-up-right](https://aka.ms/terminal)
 to run Cyberdrop-DL. Windows Terminal is the default on Windows 11.

[hashtag](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/dev/frequently-asked-questions#cyberdrop-dl-is-not-a-recognized-internal-command)

`cyberdrop-dl` is not a recognized internal command


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

This issue is caused by an improper installation of Python, specifically Python not being added to the system PATH.

It is recommended to revisit the [Getting Started](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/dev/getting-started)
 guide and follow the steps provided to reinstall or use one of the latest start scripts

[hashtag](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/dev/frequently-asked-questions#how-do-i-scrape-forum-threads)

How do I scrape forum threads?


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

You need to import cookies to use as authentication for those sites. Follow the instructions here: [How to extract cookies (DDoSGuard or login errors) #839arrow-up-right](https://github.com/jbsparrow/CyberDropDownloader/discussions/839)

[hashtag](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/dev/frequently-asked-questions#why-are-the-filenames-the-way-they-are)

Why are the filenames the way they are?


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Filenames are taken directly from the source website. Blame whoever uploaded it.

[hashtag](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/dev/frequently-asked-questions#how-do-i-fix-ssl-certificate_verify_failed)

How do I fix `[SSL: CERTIFICATE_VERIFY_FAILED]`?


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

This should only appear on macOS, so these instructions are for mac users.

Go to your applications folder, find the python folder inside of it. Run the `Install Certificates` file in that folder.

Go back to where you are running Cyberdrop-DL and delete the `venv` folder if one exists (if not, don't worry). Then try running the program again.

[hashtag](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/dev/frequently-asked-questions#a-thread-site-i-follow-has-new-posts-but-cyberdrop-dl-is-not-detecting-downloading-them-why)

A thread/site i follow has new posts but `cyberdrop-dl` is not detecting / downloading them, why?


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

`cyberdrop-dl` caches requests to made to sites to speed up re-runs and minimize load on those sites. By default, forums are cached for 30 days and any other site is cached for 7 days.

You can run with `--disable-cache` to temporarily disable the cache (CLI only) or change the default values to 0.

See:

[\--forum-cache-expire-afterarrow-up-right](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/reference/configuration-options/global-settings/rate-limiting-options#forum_cache_expire_after)

[\--file-host-cache-expire-afterarrow-up-right](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/reference/configuration-options/global-settings/rate-limiting-options#file_host_cache_expire_after)

[PreviousTransition to V8chevron-left](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/dev/upgrade)
[NextMigration to Cyberdrop-DL-Patchedchevron-right](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/dev/migration-to-cyberdrop-dl-patched)

Last updated 5 months ago

# Cyberdrop-DL Install | Cyberdrop-DL Development Docs | Cyberdrop-DL

[hashtag](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/dev/getting-started/cyberdrop-dl-install#using-start-scripts-from-release-page)

Using Start Scripts (From Release Page)


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

This is the simplest method to get the program up and running. Pre-configured start files are provided that will automatically install python, install cyberdrop-dl, update, and launch the program for you.

circle-info

The start scripts only work on 64bits operating systems. If you are running a 32bit OS, you need to install directly from pypi and may need to compile some dependencies

You can download them here: [https://github.com/jbsparrow/CyberDropDownloader/releases/latestarrow-up-right](https://github.com/jbsparrow/CyberDropDownloader/releases/latest)

You only need to download the `Cyberdrop-DL_<version>.zip` file, you don't need to worry about the other files.

Extract the contents of the zip file to any location where you'd like the program to run and store downloaded files. The extracted files will include a start file for Windows, macOS, and Linux

If you're using Windows or Linux, simply open the start file, and it will handle the rest for you

circle-info

If you are using Windows, **DO NOT** run the script as admin

On macOS, you should be able to open the start file and have everything set up automatically. However, in some rare cases, macOS users may need to run the following command first::

Copy

    xcode-select --install

chevron-rightOptional: Running Cyberdrop-DL Script with Custom Parameters[hashtag](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/dev/getting-started/cyberdrop-dl-install#optional-running-cyberdrop-dl-script-with-custom-parameters)

You can open the start script from the zip in a text editor like notepad. At the top of the file, you will this line:

Copy

    set "COMMANDLINE_ARGS="

`COMMANDLINE_ARGS`: Provide any arguments to pass to Cyberdrop-Dl. For more information, refer to the [CLI Arguments section](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/dev/reference/cli-arguments)

circle-info

You **MUST** put the values _inside_ the double quotes. Ex: `set "COMMANDLINE_ARGS=--disable-cache"`

[hashtag](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/dev/getting-started/cyberdrop-dl-install#manual-install)

Manual Install


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/dev/getting-started/cyberdrop-dl-install#id-1.-using-uv)

1\. Using `uv`

The recommended way to install Cyberdrop-DL is using [`uv`arrow-up-right](https://docs.astral.sh/uv)
.

macOS / Linux

Windows

Once you have `uv`, you can install Cyberdrop-DL using:

### 

[hashtag](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/dev/getting-started/cyberdrop-dl-install#id-2.-manual-python-install)

2\. Manual Python Install

If you do not want to or can't use `uv`, you will need to install a compatible python version manually.

If you don't have python, you can find and download it from their official website: [https://www.python.org/downloads/arrow-up-right](https://www.python.org/downloads/)

circle-info

Cyberdrop-DL requires python 3.11, 3.12 or python 3.13. The **RECOMMENDED** version is 3.12+

circle-exclamation

If you are using a version of Cyberdrop-DL from the previous repository (`cyberdrop-dl` instead of `cyberdrop-dl-patched`), you **MUST** uninstall it before installing the patched version.

Once you have python, you can install Cyberdrop-DL directly from pypi using `pipx` or `pip`. In a command prompt/terminal window:

pipx

pip

*   Install `pipx` (if you don't have it already)
    

*   Install cdl
    

circle-exclamation

Using bare `pip` to install `cyberdrop-dl-patched` is discouraged as it may lead to dependency conflicts with global installs and an inconsistent environment. Consider using `uv` or `pipx`

# UI Options | Cyberdrop-DL

[hashtag](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/reference/configuration-options/global-settings/ui-options#downloading_item_limit)

`downloading_item_limit`


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Type

Default

`PositiveInt`

`5`

This is the limit on the number of items shown in the UI (while downloading) before they are simply added to the overflow number (`and <X> other files`)

[hashtag](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/reference/configuration-options/global-settings/ui-options#refresh_rate)

`refresh_rate`


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Type

Default

`PositiveInt`

`10`

This is the refresh rate per second for the UI.

[hashtag](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/reference/configuration-options/global-settings/ui-options#scraping_item_limit)

`scraping_item_limit`


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Type

Default

`PositiveInt`

`5`

This is the limit on the number of items shown in the UI (while scraping) before they are simply added to the overflow number (`and <X> other links`)

[hashtag](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/reference/configuration-options/global-settings/ui-options#vi_mode)

`vi_mode`


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Type

Default

`bool`

`false`

This enables vi/vim key binds while editing/entering text in CDL.

# Generic Crawlers | Cyberdrop-DL

CDL has some "generic" crawlers disabled by default. Generic crawlers are designed to work on any site that uses a **specific** framework. Users can supply a list of sites to map to these crawlers, and CDL will then be able to download from them. The URL in the list should be the primary URL of the site. ex: `https://forums.docker.com/`

Supported generic crawlers:

*   `chevereto`: This works on any site that uses [Cheveretoarrow-up-right](https://chevereto.com//)
    .
    
*   `discourse`: This works on any forum that uses [Discoursearrow-up-right](https://www.discourse.org/)
    .
    
*   `wordpress_media`: This crawler should work on any [WordPressarrow-up-right](https://wordpress.com/)
     site where content primarily consists of images or galleries. The images need to be hosted on the site itself. It requires sites to have a public WordPress REST API.
    
*   `wordpress_html`: This works on any WordPress site. It scrapes the actual HTML of the site, which means it works on sites that have embedded third-party media like videos or links to hosting sites. It is always slower than `wordpress_media`.
    

[hashtag](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/reference/configuration-options/global-settings/generic_crawlers_instances#generic_crawlers_instances)

# Supported Websites | Cyberdrop-DL

For a full list of all supported sites, see [supported sites](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/reference/supported-websites#supported-sites)

[hashtag](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/reference/supported-websites#password-protected-content-hosts)

Password Protected Content Hosts


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Cyberdrop-DL can download password protected files and folders from these hosts. User must include the password as a query parameter in the input URL, adding `?password=<URL_PASSWORD>` to it.

Example: `https://cyberfile.me/folder/xUGg?password=1234`

Domain

GoFile

Cyberfile

Chevereto Sites (`JPG5`, `ImagePond.net`,`ImgLike`)

Iceyfile.com

Transfer.it

Koofr.eu

Sites supported by Real-Debrid

[hashtag](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/reference/supported-websites#additional-content-hosts-with-real-debrid)

Additional Content Hosts with Real-Debrid


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Cyberdrop-DL has integration with Real-Debrid as download service to support additional hosts. In order to enable Real-Debrid, user must provide their API token inside the `authentication.yaml` file. You can get your API token from this URL (you must be logged in): [https://real-debrid.com/apitokenarrow-up-right](https://real-debrid.com/apitoken)

Supported domains via Real-Debrid include `rapidgator`, `4shared.com`, `fikper.com`, `k2s`, `etc`. List of all supported domains can be found here (250+): [https://api.real-debrid.com/rest/1.0/hosts/domainsarrow-up-right](https://api.real-debrid.com/rest/1.0/hosts/domains)

circle-info

CDL will only use Real-Debrid for unsupported sites. To use it for a site that CDL supports, ex: `mega.nz`, you have to disable the `mega.nz` crawler. See: https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/reference/configuration-options/global-settings/general#disable\_crawlers

[hashtag](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/reference/supported-websites#supported-sites)

# General | Cyberdrop-DL

[hashtag](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/reference/configuration-options/global-settings/general#disable_crawlers)

`disable_crawlers`


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Type

Default

Additional Info

`list[NonEmptyStr]`

`[]`

This is an [`AdditiveArg`](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/reference/configuration-options/special_setting_types#additiveargs)

You can supply a list of crawlers to disable for the current run. This will make CDL completely ignore the crawler, as if the site was not supported. However, links from the site will still be processed by Real-Debrid (if enabled), Jdownloader (If enabled) and the Generic crawler (If enabled), in that order.

The list should be valid crawlers names. The name of the crawler is the name of the primary site they support. ex: `4Chan`, `Bunkrr`, `Dropbox`

Crawlers names correspond to the column `site` in the [supported sites pagearrow-up-right](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/reference/supported-websites#supported-sites)
.

[hashtag](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/reference/configuration-options/global-settings/general#enable_generic_crawler)

`enable_generic_crawler`


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Type

Default

`bool`

`false`

CDL has a generic crawler that will try to download from unsupported sites. Setting this to `true` will enable it.

circle-info

CDL will always try to download from unsupported URLs if the last part of the URL has a known file extension. ex: `.jpg`

[hashtag](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/reference/configuration-options/global-settings/general#flaresolverr)

`flaresolverr`


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Type

Default

`HttpURL` or `null`

`null`

[FlareSolverrarrow-up-right](https://github.com/FlareSolverr/FlareSolverr)
 is a proxy server to bypass Cloudflare and `DDoS-Guard` protection. The provided value must be a valid `http` URL of an existing flaresolverr instance. Ex: `http://192.168.1.44:4000`

circle-info

`0.0.0.0` is NOT a valid IP address. To set up a flaresolverr instance running on the same machine as CDL, use `127.0.0.1` as the IP

circle-exclamation

This wiki does not cover flaresolverr setup process. If you need help, refer to their documentation. Please do not open issues related to flaresolverr or `DDoS-Guard`. See: [How to extract cookies (DDoSGuard or login errors) #839arrow-up-right](https://github.com/jbsparrow/CyberDropDownloader/discussions/839)
 for alternatives using cookies

[hashtag](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/reference/configuration-options/global-settings/general#max_file_name_length)

`max_file_name_length`


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Type

Default

`PositiveInt`

`95`

This is the maximum number of characters a filename should have. CDL will truncate filenames longer that this.

[hashtag](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/reference/configuration-options/global-settings/general#max_folder_name_length)

`max_folder_name_length`


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Type

Default

`PositiveInt`

`95`

This is the maximum number of characters a folder should have. CDL will truncate folders longer that this.

[hashtag](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/reference/configuration-options/global-settings/general#proxy)

`proxy`


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Type

Default

`HttpURL` or `null`

`null`

The proxy you want CDL to use. Only `http` proxies are supported. Ex: `https://user:password@ip:port`

[hashtag](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/reference/configuration-options/global-settings/general#required_free_space)

`required_free_space`


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Type

Default

Restrictions

`ByteSize`

`5GB`

`>=512MB`

This is the minimum amount of free space require to start new downloads.

circle-info

If you set a value lower than `512MB`, CDL will override it with `512MB`

[hashtag](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/reference/configuration-options/global-settings/general#ssl_context)

`ssl_context`


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Type

Default

`NonEmptyStr` or None

`truststore+certifi`

Context that will used to verify SSL connections. Valid values are:

*   `truststore`: Will use certificates already included with the OS
    
*   `certifi`: Will use certificates bundled with the `certifi` version available at the release of the current CDL version
    
*   `truststore+certifi`: Will use certificates already included with the OS, with a fallback to `certifi` for missing certificates
    
*   `None`: Will completely disable SSL verification, allowing insecure connections.
    

Setting this to `None` will allow the program to connect to websites without SSL encryption (insecurely).

triangle-exclamation

Sensitive data may be exposed using an insecure connection. For your safety, is recommended to always use a secure HTTPS connection.

[hashtag](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/reference/configuration-options/global-settings/general#user_agent)

`user_agent`


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Type

Default

`NonEmptyStr`

`Mozilla/5.0 (Windows NT 10.0; Win64; x64; rv:142.0) Gecko/20100101 Firefox/142.0`

The user agent is the signature of your browser. Some sites use it to identify if the requests come from a human or a robot. You can google "what is my user agent" to get yours.

circle-info

If you use flaresolverr, this value MUST match with flaresolverr's user agent. Otherwise, flaresolverr cookies won't work

[PreviousGlobal Settingschevron-left](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/reference/configuration-options/global-settings)
[NextRate Limiting Optionschevron-right](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/reference/configuration-options/global-settings/rate-limiting-options)

Last updated 5 months ago

*   [flaresolverr](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/reference/configuration-options/global-settings/general#flaresolverr)
    
*   [max\_file\_name\_length](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/reference/configuration-options/global-settings/general#max_file_name_length)
    
*   [max\_folder\_name\_length](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/reference/configuration-options/global-settings/general#max_folder_name_length)

# Media Duration Limits | Cyberdrop-DL

You can provide the maximum and minimum duration for audio and video files.

Type

Default

`timedelta`

`0s`

*   A `timedelta` input is expected to be a valid ISO 8601 timespan, ex: `P10DT2H30M10S`
    
*   An `int` input is assumed to be the number of days
    
*   A `str` input is expected to be in the format; `<value> <unit>`, ex: `10 days`.
    

Setting any of these options to `0` means that limit is `disabled`

*   `minimum_audio_duration`
    
*   `maximum_audio_duration`
    
*   `minimum_video_duration`
    
*   `maximum_video_duration`

# Rate Limiting Options | Cyberdrop-DL

[hashtag](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/reference/configuration-options/global-settings/rate-limiting-options#connection_timeout)

`connection_timeout`


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Type

Default

`PositiveInt`

`15`

The number of seconds to wait while connecting to a website before timing out

circle-info

This value will also be used for Flaresolverr (if enabled) as the max number of seconds to solve a CAPTCHA challenge

[hashtag](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/reference/configuration-options/global-settings/rate-limiting-options#download_attempts)

`download_attempts`


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Type

Default

`PositiveInt`

`2`

The number of download attempts per file. Some conditions are never retried (such as a `404` HTTP status)

[hashtag](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/reference/configuration-options/global-settings/rate-limiting-options#download_delay)

`download_delay`


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Type

Default

`NonNegativeFloat`

`0.0`

This is the number of seconds to wait between downloads to the same domain.

Some domains have internal limits set by the program, which can not be modified:

*   `bunkr`: 0.5
    
*   `coomer`: 0.5
    
*   `kemono`: 0.5
    
*   `nhentai.net`: 1
    

[hashtag](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/reference/configuration-options/global-settings/rate-limiting-options#download_speed_limit)

`download_speed_limit`


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Type

Default

`ByteSize`

`0`

circle-info

This setting specifies speed and it's interpreted as `<value> / second`. ex: `8MB` means `8MB/s`

This is the max rate of downloading in bytes (per second) for all downloads combined. Set to `0` to disable

[hashtag](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/reference/configuration-options/global-settings/rate-limiting-options#file_host_cache_expire_after)

`file_host_cache_expire_after`


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Type

Default

`timedelta`, `str` or `int`

`7 days`

Cyberdrop-DL caches the requests made to any website. This setting controls how long responses to file host websites are stored before expiring.

*   A `timedelta` input is expected to be a valid ISO 8601 timespan, ex: `P10DT2H30M10S`
    
*   An `int` input is assumed to be the number of days
    
*   A `str` input is expected to be in the format; `<value> <unit>`, ex: `10 days`.
    

### 

[hashtag](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/reference/configuration-options/global-settings/rate-limiting-options#valid-str-units)

Valid `str` units

*   `year(s)`
    
*   `month(s)`
    
*   `week(s)`
    
*   `day(s)`
    
*   `hour(s)`
    
*   `minute(s)`
    
*   `second(s)`
    
*   `millisecond(s)`
    
*   `microsecond(s)`
    

circle-info

You can set the value to `0` to disable caching

[hashtag](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/reference/configuration-options/global-settings/rate-limiting-options#forum_cache_expire_after)

`forum_cache_expire_after`


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Type

Default

`timedelta`, `str` or `int`

`4 weeks`

Same as `file_host_cache_expire_after` but applied to forums requests.

[hashtag](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/reference/configuration-options/global-settings/rate-limiting-options#jitter)

`jitter`


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Type

Default

`NonNegativeFloat`

`0.0`

Additional number of seconds to wait in between downloads. CDL will wait an additional random number of seconds in between 0 and the `jitter` value.

[hashtag](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/reference/configuration-options/global-settings/rate-limiting-options#max_simultaneous_downloads)

`max_simultaneous_downloads`


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Type

Default

`PositiveInt`

`15`

This is the maximum number of files that can be downloaded simultaneously.

[hashtag](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/reference/configuration-options/global-settings/rate-limiting-options#max_simultaneous_downloads_per_domain)

`max_simultaneous_downloads_per_domain`


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Type

Default

`PositiveInt`

`5`

This is the maximum number of files that can be downloaded from a single domain simultaneously.

Some domains have internal limits set by the program, which can not be modified:

*   `bunkr`: 1 per unique server
    
*   `cyberdrop`: 1
    
*   `cyberfile`: 1
    
*   `noodlemagazine`: 2
    
*   `4chan`: 1
    
*   `pixeldrain`: 2
    
*   `xxxbunker`: 2
    

[hashtag](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/reference/configuration-options/global-settings/rate-limiting-options#rate_limit)

`rate_limit`


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Type

Default

`PositiveFloat`

`50.0`

circle-info

This setting specifies speed and it's interpreted as `<value> / second`. ex: `50` means `50 requests / second`

This is the maximum number of requests that can be made by the program per second.

[hashtag](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/reference/configuration-options/global-settings/rate-limiting-options#read_timeout)

`read_timeout`


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Type

Default

`PositiveFloat` or `null`

`300.0`

The number of seconds to wait while reading data from a website before timing out. A `null` value will make CDL keep the socket connection open indefinitely, even if the server is not sending data anymore

[PreviousGeneralchevron-left](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/reference/configuration-options/global-settings/general)
[NextUI Optionschevron-right](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/reference/configuration-options/global-settings/ui-options)

Last updated 3 months ago

# Special Type Options | Cyberdrop-DL Development Docs | Cyberdrop-DL

[hashtag](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/dev/reference/configuration-options/special_setting_types#additiveargs)

`AdditiveArgs`


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Special type for some settings that accept multiple values as input (`lists` or `sets`). When passing values as CLI arguments, if the first value is `+`, any value after it will be added to the values specified in the config file instead of overriding it. Similarly, if the first value is `-`, any value after it will be removed from the values specified in the config

### 

[hashtag](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/dev/reference/configuration-options/special_setting_types#examples)

Examples

If you have the following `skip_hosts` setting in you config file:

Copy

    skip_hosts:
      - drive.google.com
      - youtube.com
      - facebook.com

You will get the following results:

Value you used

Value CDL interpreted

Details

`--skip-hosts instagram.com`

`[instagram.com]`

config values were overridden by CLI values

`--skip-hosts "+" instagram.com`

`[drive.google.com, youtube.com, facebook.com, instagram.com]`

config values and CLI values were merged

`--skip-hosts "-" drive.google.com youtube.com`

`[facebook.com]`

CLI values were removed from the config values

circle-info

Always use quotes for "+" and "-" to make sure your shell does not try to parse them as additional flags

[hashtag](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/dev/reference/configuration-options/special_setting_types#boolflag)

`BoolFlag`


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

A special kind of `bool`. Within a config file, it can have a `true` or `false` value. However, when used via CLI, the value is assumed from the flag name. The normal name is `true`, and prefixing the name with `--no` means `false`.

### 

[hashtag](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/dev/reference/configuration-options/special_setting_types#examples-1)

Examples

Value you used

Value CDL interpreted

`--auto-dedupe`

auto-dedupe: `true`

`--no-auto-dedupe`

auto-dedupe: `false`

[hashtag](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/dev/reference/configuration-options/special_setting_types#bytesize)

`ByteSize`


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

A special kind of `int` that also accepts suffixes like `GB`, `MiB` and `KB` to specify valid values

In conformance with IEC 80000-13 Standard, `1KB` means `1000 bytes`, and `1KiB` means `1024 bytes`. In general, including a middle 'i' will cause the unit to be interpreted as a power of 2, rather than a power of 10.

### 

[hashtag](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/dev/reference/configuration-options/special_setting_types#examples-2)

Examples

Value you used

Value CDL interpreted

`1GB`

`1.000.000.000 bytes`

`512`

`512 bytes`

`1MiB`

`1.048.576 bytes`

circle-info

`ByteSize` is also used for some settings to specify speed and it's interpreted as `<value> / second`. ex: `8MB` means `8MB/s`

[PreviousConfiguration Optionschevron-left](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/dev/reference/configuration-options)
[NextAuthenticationchevron-right](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/dev/reference/configuration-options/authentication)

Last updated 5 months ago

*   [AdditiveArgs](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/dev/reference/configuration-options/special_setting_types#additiveargs)
    
*   [Examples](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/dev/reference/configuration-options/special_setting_types#examples)
    
*   [BoolFlag](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/dev/reference/configuration-options/special_setting_types#boolflag)
    
*   [Examples](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/dev/reference/configuration-options/special_setting_types#examples-1)
    
*   [ByteSize](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/dev/reference/configuration-options/special_setting_types#bytesize)
    
*   [Examples](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/dev/reference/configuration-options/special_setting_types#examples-2)

# Configuration Options | Cyberdrop-DL Development Docs | Cyberdrop-DL

There are three type of config files: config settings, global settings and authentication settings.

[user-lockAuthenticationchevron-right](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/dev/reference/configuration-options/authentication)
[earth-americasGlobal Settingschevron-right](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/dev/reference/configuration-options/global-settings)
[screwdriver-wrenchSettingschevron-right](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/dev/reference/configuration-options/settings)

circle-info

**Global Settings** and **Authentication Settings** are "global". They apply to _all_ config settings. You can set them once and never touch them again.

Each config setting will be setup by default to have a separate `URLs.txt` files and separate log files.

[PreviousSupported Websiteschevron-left](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/dev/reference/supported-websites)
[NextSpecial Type Optionschevron-right](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/dev/reference/configuration-options/special_setting_types)

Last updated 3 months ago

sun-brightdesktopmoon

sun-brightdesktopmoon

---

# CLI Arguments | Cyberdrop-DL

circle-info

CLI inputs always take priority over config values.

circle-info

Use `-` instead of `_` to separate words in an config option name when using it as a CLI argument: Ex: `auto_dedupe` needs to be `auto-dedupe` when using it via the CLI

You can pass any of the **Config Settings** and **Global Settings** options as a cli argument for the program.

For items not explained below, you can find their counterparts in the configuration options to see what they do.

[hashtag](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/reference/cli-arguments#cli-only-arguments)

CLI only arguments


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/reference/cli-arguments#appdata-folder)

`appdata-folder`

Type

Default

`Path`

`<Current Working Directory>`

Folder where Cyberdrop-DL will store it's database, cache and config files.

### 

[hashtag](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/reference/cli-arguments#completed-after)

`completed-after`

Type

Default

`date`

`None`

Only retry downloads that were completed on or after this date. The date should be in ISO 8601 format, for example, `2021-12-23`

circle-info

This option has no effect unless you run CDL with `--retry-all`

### 

[hashtag](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/reference/cli-arguments#completed-before)

`completed-before`

Type

Default

`date`

`None`

Only retry downloads that were completed on or before this date. The date should be in ISO 8601 format, for example, `2021-12-23`

circle-info

This option has no effect unless you run CDL with `--retry-all`

### 

[hashtag](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/reference/cli-arguments#config)

`config`

Type

Default

`str`

`None`

Name of config to load. Use `ALL` to run all configs sequentially

### 

[hashtag](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/reference/cli-arguments#config-file)

`config-file`

Type

Default

`Path`

`None`

Path to the CDL `settings.yaml` file to load

circle-info

If both `config` and `config-file` are supplied, `config-file` takes priority

### 

[hashtag](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/reference/cli-arguments#disable-cache)

`disable-cache`

Type

Default

Action

`BoolFlag`

`False`

`store_true`

Disables read/writes to requests cache for the current run only. All config settings or arguments related to the cache (ex: `file_host_cache_expire_after`) will be ignored.

### 

[hashtag](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/reference/cli-arguments#download)

`download`

Type

Default

Action

`BoolFlag`

`False`

`store_true`

Skips UI, start download immediately

### 

[hashtag](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/reference/cli-arguments#download-tiktok-audios)

`download-tiktok-audios`

Type

Default

Action

`BoolFlag`

`False`

`store_true`

Download TikTok audios from posts and save them as separate files

### 

[hashtag](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/reference/cli-arguments#download-tiktok-src-quality-videos)

`download-tiktok-src-quality-videos`

Type

Default

Action

`BoolFlag`

`False`

`store_true`

By default, CDL will download the "optimized for streaming" version of tiktok videos. Setting this option to `True` will download videos in original (source) quality.

`_original` will be added as a suffix to their filename.

circle-exclamation

This will make video downloads several times slower

When it is set to `False` (the default) CDL can download 50 videos with a single request. When it is set to `True` , CDL needs to make at least 3 requests _per_ video to download them.

There's also a daily limit of the API CDL uses: 5000 requests per day per IP

Setting this option to `True` will consume the daily limit faster

### 

[hashtag](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/reference/cli-arguments#impersonate)

`impersonate`

Type

Default

Action

`chrome", "edge", "safari", "safari_ios", "chrome_android", "firefox"`, `BoolFlag` or `null`

`null`

`store_true` or `store_const`

Impersonation allows CDL to make requests and appear to be a legitimate web browser. This helps bypass bot-protection on some sites and it's required for any site that only accepts HTTP2 connections.

*   The default value (`null`) means CDL will automatically use impersonation for crawlers that were programmed to use it.
    
*   Passing the flag without any value (`--impersonate`) is the same as `--impersonate True`: CDL will use impersonation for ALL requests, using the default impersonation target
    
*   Passing an specific target (ex: `--impersonate chrome_android`) will make CDL use impersonation for all requests, using that tarjet
    

circle-info

The current default target is `chrome`. The default target can change on any new release without notice

### 

[hashtag](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/reference/cli-arguments#max-items-retry)

`max-items-retry`

Type

Default

`NonNegativeInt`

`0`

Max number of links to retry. Using `0` means no limit

circle-info

This option has no effect unless you run CDL with one of the retry options: `--retry-all`, `--retry-failed` or `--retry-maintenance`

### 

[hashtag](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/reference/cli-arguments#portrait)

`portrait`

Type

Default

Action

`BoolFlag`

`False`

`store_true`

Force CDL to run with a vertical layout

### 

[hashtag](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/reference/cli-arguments#print-stats)

`print-stats`

Type

Default

Action

`BoolFlag`

`True`

`store_false`

Show stats report at the end of a run

### 

[hashtag](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/reference/cli-arguments#retry-all)

`retry-all`

Type

Default

Action

`BoolFlag`

`False`

`store_true`

Retry all downloads

### 

[hashtag](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/reference/cli-arguments#retry-failed)

`retry-failed`

Type

Default

Action

`BoolFlag`

`False`

`store_true`

Retry failed downloads

### 

[hashtag](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/reference/cli-arguments#retry-maintenance)

`retry-maintenance`

Type

Default

Action

`BoolFlag`

`False`

`store_true`

Retry download of maintenance files (bunkr). Requires files to be hashed

### 

[hashtag](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/reference/cli-arguments#show-supported-sites)

`show-supported-sites`

Type

Default

Action

`BoolFlag`

`False`

`store_true`

Shows a list of all supported sites and exits

### 

[hashtag](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/reference/cli-arguments#ui)

`ui`

Type

Default

`CaseInsensitiveStrEnum`

`FULLSCREEN`

UI can have 1 of these values:

*   `DISABLED` : no output at all
    
*   `ACTIVITY` : only shows a spinner with the text `running CDL...`
    
*   `SIMPLE`: shows spinner + simplified progress bar
    
*   `FULLSCREEN`: shows the normal UI/progress view
    

circle-info

Values are case insensitive, ex: both `disabled` and `DISABLED` are valid

[hashtag](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/reference/cli-arguments#overview)

Overview


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Bool arguments like options within `Download Options`, `Ignore Options`, `Runtime Options`, etc. can be prefixed with `--no-` to negate them. Ex: `--no-auto-dedupe` will disable auto dedupe, overriding whatever the config option was set to.

[PreviousGeneric Crawlerschevron-left](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/reference/configuration-options/global-settings/generic_crawlers_instances)
[NextNotificationschevron-right](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/reference/notifications)

# Authentication | Cyberdrop-DL Development Docs | Cyberdrop-DL

All the options in these list are optional. The default value for all of them is an empty `str`

Type

Default

`str`

`""`

chevron-rightCoomer[hashtag](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/dev/reference/configuration-options/authentication#coomer)

*   `session`
    

Value of the `session` cookie from the website. This will allow CDL to download from your favoruites by using `https://coomer.st/favorites` as an input URL.

chevron-rightKemono[hashtag](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/dev/reference/configuration-options/authentication#kemono)

*   `session`
    

Value of the `session` cookie from the website. This will allow CDL to download from your favoruites by using `https://kemono.cr/favorites` as an input URL.

chevron-rightForums[hashtag](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/dev/reference/configuration-options/authentication#forums)

circle-exclamation

Logging to forums with `Authentication` was deprecated in v6.7.0

You need to use cookie files.

See: [How to extract cookies (DDoSGuard or login errors) #839arrow-up-right](https://github.com/jbsparrow/CyberDropDownloader/discussions/839)

chevron-rightGoFile[hashtag](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/dev/reference/configuration-options/authentication#gofile)

If you decide to pay for GoFile Premium (faster downloads, etc.) you can provide your API key to Cyberdrop-DL in order for the program to use it.

*   `api_key`
    

You can get your API key here: [https://gofile.io/myProfilearrow-up-right](https://gofile.io/myProfile)

chevron-rightJDownloader[hashtag](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/dev/reference/configuration-options/authentication#jdownloader)

Under JDownloader 2 settings -> MyJDownloader:

*   `username`
    
*   `password`
    
*   `device`
    

chevron-rightPixelDrain[hashtag](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/dev/reference/configuration-options/authentication#pixeldrain)

If you decide to pay for PixelDrain premium (faster downloads, etc.) you can provide your API key to Cyberdrop-DL in order for the program to use it.

*   `api_key`
    

You can get your API key here: [https://pixeldrain.com/user/api\_keysarrow-up-right](https://pixeldrain.com/user/api_keys)

chevron-rightReal-Debrid[hashtag](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/dev/reference/configuration-options/authentication#real-debrid)

In order to download files from sites supported by real-debrid, you'll need to get the API token from your account.

*   `api_key`
    

You can get your API key here (you must be logged in): [https://real-debrid.com/apitokenarrow-up-right](https://real-debrid.com/apitoken)

chevron-rightMega.nz[hashtag](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/dev/reference/configuration-options/authentication#mega.nz)

If you have premium or want to download files/folders only shared with you, provide CDL these values:

*   `email`
    
*   `password`
    

circle-exclamation

Accounts with 2 factor authentication (2FA) are NOT supported

# Logs | Cyberdrop-DL

[hashtag](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/reference/configuration-options/settings/logs#download_error_urls)

`download_error_urls`


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Type

Default

Restrictions

`Path`

`Download_Error_URLs.csv`

extension will always be overridden to `.csv`

Path of the download error log. For relative paths, the final path will be `log_folder` / `download_error_urls`

Cyberdrop-DL will output the links it fails to download, the reason and their origin in CSV format.

[hashtag](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/reference/configuration-options/settings/logs#last_forum_post)

`last_forum_post`


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Type

Default

Restrictions

`Path`

`Last_Scraped_Forum_Posts.csv`

extension will always be overridden to `.csv`

Path of the forum-post log file. For relative paths, the final path will be `log_folder` / `last_forum_post`

Cyberdrop-DL will store the link to the last forum posts it scraped from a given forum thread in this file.

[hashtag](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/reference/configuration-options/settings/logs#log_folder)

`log_folder`


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Type

Default

`Path`

`AppData/Configs/{config}/Logs`

The path to the location you want Cyberdrop-DL to store logs in.

[hashtag](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/reference/configuration-options/settings/logs#log_line_width)

`log_line_width`


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Type

Default

Restrictions

`PositiveInt`

`240`

`>=50`

Line width to use when writing to the main log file

[hashtag](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/reference/configuration-options/settings/logs#logs_expire_after)

`logs_expire_after`


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Type

Default

`timedelta` or `null`

`null`

With `rotate_logs` enabled, this setting specifies the retention period for log files before they are deleted.

*   A `timedelta` input is expected to be a valid ISO 8601 timespan, ex: `P10DT2H30M10S`
    
*   An `int` input is assumed to be the number of days
    
*   A `str` input is expected to be in the format; `<value> <unit>`, ex: `10 days`.
    
*   A `null` value means disabled (never delete any logs)
    

circle-exclamation

Any `.log` or `.csv` file within `log_folder` will be deleted, even if CDL did not create them

circle-info

Log files with an absolute path not relative to `log_folder` will never be deleted

[hashtag](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/reference/configuration-options/settings/logs#main_log)

`main_log`


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Type

Default

Restrictions

`Path`

`downloader.log`

extension will always be overridden to `.log`

Path of main log file. For relative paths, the final path will be `log_folder` / `main_log`

[hashtag](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/reference/configuration-options/settings/logs#rotate_logs)

`rotate_logs`


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Type

Default

`bool`

`false`

If enabled, Cyberdrop-DL will add the current date and time as a suffix to each log file, in the format `YYMMDD_HHMMSS`

Every log file will be created inside a sub folder with the current date

This will prevent overriding old log files

[hashtag](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/reference/configuration-options/settings/logs#scrape_error_urls)

`scrape_error_urls`


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Type

Default

Restrictions

`Path`

`Scrape_Error_URLs.csv`

extension will always be overridden to `.csv`

What you want Cyberdrop-DL to call the scrape error log. For relative paths, the final path will be `log_folder` / `scrape_error_urls`

Cyberdrop-DL will output the links it fails to scrape, the reason and their origin in CSV format.

[hashtag](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/reference/configuration-options/settings/logs#unsupported_urls)

`unsupported_urls`


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Type

Default

Restrictions

`Path`

`Unsupported_URLs.csv`

extension will always be overridden to `.csv`

Path of the unsupported log file. For relative paths, the final path will be `log_folder` / `unsupported_urls`

Cyberdrop-DL will output links it can't download to this file.

[hashtag](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/reference/configuration-options/settings/logs#webhook)

`webhook`


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Type

Default

Restrictions

`AppriseURL` or `null`

`null`

The scheme of the URL must be `http` or `https`

The URL of a webhook that you want to send download stats to (Ex: Discord). You can add the optional tag `attach_logs=` as a prefix to include a copy of the main log as an attachment.

Example:

> `attach_logs=https://discord.com/api/webhooks/webhook_id/webhook_token`

# Dupe Cleanup Options | Cyberdrop-DL Development Docs | Cyberdrop-DL

Cyberdrop-DL maintains an internal database of all downloaded files, indexed by their hashes. This can be used to automatically delete newly downloaded files if they were downloaded before. To enable auto dupe cleanup:

1.  Set `hashing` to `IN_PLACE` or `POST_DOWNLOAD`
    
2.  Set `auto_dedupe` to `true`
    

[hashtag](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/dev/reference/configuration-options/settings/dupe_cleanup_options#add_md5_hash)

`add_md5_hash`


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Type

Default

`bool`

`false`

If enabled, calculates the `md5` hash for every downloaded file and store it in the internal database. This allows the program to match files with sites that provide hash information before downloading them, skipping the download altogether if a match is found

circle-info

`md5` was the default hashing algorithm of Cyberdrop-DL V5. Since v6, the default algorithm is `xxhash128`.

[hashtag](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/dev/reference/configuration-options/settings/dupe_cleanup_options#add_sha256_hash)

`add_sha256_hash`


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Type

Default

`bool`

`false`

If enabled, calculates the `sha256` hash for every downloaded file and store it in the internal database. This allows the program to match files with sites that provide hash information before downloading them, skipping the download altogether if a match is found

[hashtag](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/dev/reference/configuration-options/settings/dupe_cleanup_options#auto_dedupe)

`auto_dedupe`


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Type

Default

`bool`

`false`

Enables deduping files functionality. Needs `hashing` to be enabled

The `auto_dedupe` feature scans the database for files with matching hashes and sizes, automatically deleting any duplicates and retaining only the oldest copy.

Deletion will only occur if two or more matching files are found during the database search.

circle-exclamation

Auto dedupe will delete files if you have _ever_ downloaded them before, even if you no longer have the original download on disk

[hashtag](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/dev/reference/configuration-options/settings/dupe_cleanup_options#hashing)

`hashing`


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Type

Default

Restrictions

`HASHING`

`OFF`

Must be `OFF`, `IN_PLACE` or `POST_DOWNLOAD`

There are three possible options for hashing:

1.  `OFF`: disables hashing
    
2.  `IN_PLACE`: performs hashing after each download
    
3.  `POST_DOWNLOAD`: performs hashing after all downloads have completed
    

The default hashing algorithm is `xxh128`. You can enable additional hashing algorithms, but you can not replace the default.

[hashtag](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/dev/reference/configuration-options/settings/dupe_cleanup_options#send_deleted_to_trash)

`send_deleted_to_trash`


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Type

Default

`bool`

`false`

Deduped files are sent to the trash bin instead of being deleted

[PreviousDownload Optionschevron-left](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/dev/reference/configuration-options/settings/download_options)
[NextFile Size Limitschevron-right](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/dev/reference/configuration-options/settings/file_size_limits)

Last updated 5 months ago

*   [add\_sha256\_hash](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/dev/reference/configuration-options/settings/dupe_cleanup_options#add_sha256_hash)

# Sorting | Cyberdrop-DL

Cyberdrop-DL has a file sorter built in, but it's disabled by default

You can use the field names below to create a custom path format. You can also use essentially none of them and have a hard coded path. However, `filename` and `ext` must always be used.

Common fields for sorting format options (supported for `audio`, `videos`, `images` and `other`):

> `base_dir`: the name of highest level folder inside `scan_folder`. This normally is the model name or the thread name
> 
> `ext`: the file extension (suffix)
> 
> `file_date`: the file date. This is a datetime object, which means it accepts a custom format spec ex: `{file_date:%Y-%m}`
> 
> `file_date_iso`: the file date as an iso 8601 string (`%Y-%m-%d`)
> 
> `file_date_us`: the file date in the US format (`%Y-%d-%m`)
> 
> `filename`: the file's name (stem)
> 
> `parent_dir`: the name of the folder where the file is located at (its parent folder). This is normally the album name for photos or the post name for forums/reddit if `separate_post` is enabled
> 
> `sort_dir`: the same path as `sort_folder` from the download options

[hashtag](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/reference/configuration-options/settings/sorting#scan_folder)

`scan_folder`


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Type

Default

`Path` or `null`

`null`

Sets the starting point for the file scan

Each direct child of the `scan_folder` is recursively scanned, and files are moved based on your settings.

If this is set to `null` (the default), the value of `download_dir` from the download options is used.

[hashtag](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/reference/configuration-options/settings/sorting#sort_downloads)

`sort_downloads`


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Type

Default

`bool`

`false`

Setting this to `true` will allow Cyberdrop-DL to sort downloads after a run is complete.

[hashtag](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/reference/configuration-options/settings/sorting#sort_folder)

`sort_folder`


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Type

Default

`Path`

`Downloads/Cyberdrop-DL Sorted Downloads`

This is the path to the folder you'd like sorted downloads to be stored in.

circle-exclamation

Setting `sort_folder` to the same value as `scan_folder` is not supported and will lead to expected results

[hashtag](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/reference/configuration-options/settings/sorting#sort_incrementer_format)

`sort_incrementer_format`


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Type

Default

`NonEmptyStr`

`({i})`

When naming collisions happen, Cyberdrop-DL will rename files automatically

> `image.jpg` -> `image (1).jpg`.

You can modify the format as needed, but it must include `{i}` to specify where the auto-increment value should be placed

[hashtag](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/reference/configuration-options/settings/sorting#sorted_audio)

`sorted_audio`


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Type

Default

`NonEmptyStr` or `null`

`{sort_dir}/{base_dir}/Audio/{filename}{ext}`

This is the format for the directory structure and naming scheme for audio files. Set to `null` to skip sorting audio files

In addition to the common sorting format fields, this option supports:

> `bitrate`: file bit rate. This is an `int`
> 
> `duration`: audio total runtime in seconds. This is an `int`
> 
> `length`: same as `duration`
> 
> `sample_rate`: audio sample rate. This is an `int`

[hashtag](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/reference/configuration-options/settings/sorting#sorted_image)

`sorted_image`


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Type

Default

`NonEmptyStr` or `null`

`{sort_dir}/{base_dir}/Images/{filename}{ext}`

This is the format for the directory structure and naming scheme for image files. Set to `null` to skip sorting image files

In addition to the common sorting format fields, this option supports:

> `height`: vertical pixel count. This is an `int`
> 
> `width`: horizontal pixel count. This is an `int`
> 
> `resolution`: `width`x`height` ex. 1080x1920. This is a `str`

[hashtag](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/reference/configuration-options/settings/sorting#sorted_video)

`sorted_video`


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Type

Default

`NonEmptyStr` or `null`

`{sort_dir}/{base_dir}/Video/{filename}{ext}`

This is the format for the directory structure and naming scheme for video files. Set to `null` to skip sorting video files

In addition to the common sorting format fields, this option supports:

> `codec`: ex. h264. This is a `str`. It could potentially be `None` for some files
> 
> `duration`: video total runtime in seconds. This is an `int`
> 
> `fps`: ex. `24`. This represents a number but is a `str`. It could potentially be `None` for some files
> 
> `length`: same as `duration`
> 
> `height`: vertical pixel count. This is an `int`
> 
> `width`: horizontal pixel count.This is an `int`
> 
> `resolution`: `width`x`height` ex. 1080x1920. This is a `str`

[hashtag](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/reference/configuration-options/settings/sorting#sorted_other)

`sorted_other`


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Type

Default

`NonEmptyStr` or `null`

`{sort_dir}/{base_dir}/Other/{filename}{ext}`

This is the format for the directory structure and naming scheme for other files. Set to `null` to skip sorting other files

[hashtag](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/reference/configuration-options/settings/sorting#group-urls)

Group URLs


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

It is possible to treat a list of URLs as a group, allowing them to be downloaded to a single folder.

To define a group, put a title above the URLs you want to be in the group, using the format: `--- <group_name>` or `=== <group_name>`.

To define the end of a group, add a new group with no name. (`---` or `===`)

Here is an example URL file with two groups:

Those downloads would be sorted as follows:

Loose Files

Group 1

Group 2

file1.jpg

file2.jpg

file5.jpg

file4.jpg

file3.jpg

file6.jpg

file7.jpg

[NextGlobal Settingschevron-right](https://script-ware.gitbook.io/cyberdrop-dl/reference/configuration-options/global-settings)
